                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 LA RAMS Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The LA RAMS GROUP is for fans of the Los Angeles Rams NFL football team. This group is for passionate Rams fans that want to contribute ideas, news, questions, insight, and lively conversation regarding The LA RAMS or football in general. Other topics of importance may be discussed in this group as well. Consider it the thinking fans Rams Groups. In order for the continued success of this fast growing group there are a few rules necessary to be implemented. (1) Hateful, vulgar, and harmful speech will not be tolerated. Personal attacks because of gender, sexual orientation, nationality, LOCATION, physical characteristics or mental limitations are not welcomed. (2) No "Who Cares" comments - unless you are posting information that you do care about. If you don't care then move onto a post that you do care about or STFU!!! (3) Members are not allowed to block administrators or moderators. (4) No bullying of any kind will be tolerated. Physical threats will be promptly handled without warning with immediate expulsion. (5) Fake profile’s request for membership will be denied. (6) No advertising other groups in this group. No selling of any products without consent from administrators or moderators. (7) Any kind of pornography will be quickly reported and deleted. Unless it's really good then PM me immediately 🤣🤣🤣 (8) Please contribute to the group when possible. Post and comment and if you don't like a post move onto the next one and post things that interest you regarding the rams. *If you see any of the above rules being broken or a post unrelated to the LA RAMS or football please report the post by clicking on the upper right hand side of the post or contacting one the group admins or moderator -Work with us to make this group an enjoyable experience. Please feel free to invite your friends and family to join our "Ramily" as we look forward to the 2020 season of Los Angeles Rams football. GO RAMS!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 College Gymnastics Alumni
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is to share pretty much anything with each other! Our post gym transition struggles/successes, life advice, professional advice, job sharing/searching, general fitness thoughts/ideas/workouts etc. Basically anything you could think of! After joining the group, please respond to the message an admin sends you! This group is open to any female gymnast who participated in college gymnastics! Only rules are you have to be graduated to be a part of the group. Code of Conduct: 1. Positivity only! This group is to lift each other up and encourage us. 2. Keep it drama free please! No gossip. 3. Be vulnerable; it's how we grow and help others! "To share your weakness is to make yourself vulnerable; to make yourself vulnerable is to show your strength." 4. Trust me, you aren't the only one struggling with something. Bring it up even if it's awkward or you think it's strange. Share what you're going through. 5. Please only share things that happened to you or that you've had experience with... don't share another person's experience that they have shared with you unless you have their permission. 6. Lastly, make connections! Find people around you. Get to know them. Community is so important and it's hard without it. Let's face it, few people actually understand what we went through to this point in our lives. Find people who understand and that you can share life with! That's not to say other people can't understand, but it's always nice to have someone who also went through it! 
                </div>

This means we have the ability to speak kind, positive words that build one another up. Profanity only destructs the ability to have a civilized conversation and only promotes and brings negative effect within the group and towards those who it is directed towards. -No indecent images. We try to keep with the theme here. We welcome pictures from Dodgers fans. We do not welcome images that promote sex, drugs or harm to one another. We try to keep this a safe place for Dodgers fans of all ages. -No selling unless permission is given. We understand that this a Dodgers group and understand that Dodgers fans have great things to share. We aim to prevent spamming by making this one of our rules. -Keep posts Dodgers related. We desire to bring Dodgers fans together and promote connection This is a Dodgers group. Keep that in mind. If you have an issue with anything please pm an admin. It saves our admins the trouble of deleting someone's distressing comment that could have been addressed on a more individual level. This is a Dodgers group and we love our Dodgers fans here.              <h2 class="_8tjp _8usa _8us0 _8us1">开启小组对话</h2>
             <div class="mvm uiP _8tjq fsm">

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Los Angeles Rams
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 http://www.superbrawl.com/pools.php?wppk1022 Rams Club https://www.facebook.com/groups/RamsClub/ Los Angeles Rams 2016-Present ST. Louis Rams 1995-2015 Los Angeles Rams 1946-1994, Cleveland Rams 1937-1945 NFL Champions 1945, 1951, Super Bowl XXXIV. The Rams started as the Cleveland Rams from 1937-1945 and then moved to Los Angeles 1946-1994. The Rams won their first NFL Championship in 1945 with quarterback Bob Waterfield. 1946: The Los Angeles Rams proved to be ahead of their time right away as they signed halfback Kenny Washington, and WR Woody Strode. The two became the first black players to play in the NFL since the NFL instituted a ban on black players in 1932. In 1948, tailback Fred Gehrke, painted gold horns on blue leather helmets, and all the other teams soon followed with their team logos. L.A. Rams won their second NFL Championship In 1951 with Quarterbacks Bob Waterfield and Norm Van Brocklin, and were Western Division Champions in 1949, and National Conference Champions in 1950, 51 &amp; 55. The Los Angeles Rams were Coastal Division Champions in 1967 &amp; 1969, and NFC Western Division Champions 1973, 74, 75, 76, 77, 78, 79, 85, &amp; 1999. Rams were NFC Champions in 1979, 1999 &amp; 2001. in 1979, the Los Angeles Rams lost Superbowl XIV to the Pittsburgh Steelers with backup Quarterback Vince Ferragamo. The St. Louis Rams 1995-2015, beat the Tennessee Titans 23-16 and won SuperBowl XXXIV in 1999, with backup Quarterback Kurt Warner. Linebacker Mike Jones made probably the most famous game winning "The Tackle" in NFL history, to stop the Titans receiver just short of the goal line, on the last play of the game. In 2001, the Rams lost SuperBowl XXXVI to the New England Patriots with Quarterback Kurt Warner.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ANGELS FANS 4 LIFE
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the #1 Angels fan group where we support our team 24/7 ☞ Please feel free to invite friends or family and post about anything Angels related. ☞ Please avoid excessive criticism of the team or any comments that instigate strife with other members. ☞ Keep ALL game related comments to the Game Thread, located under "View Pinned Post" (Personal pictures from the game can still be posted to the group) ☞ NO SALES OR ADVERTISING/PROMOTION ALLOWED (If you are from a nonprofit organization please message one of the admins for approval to post your link to the group) ☞If you'd like to sell Angels related items you can join our AF4L Marketplace: https://www.facebook.com/groups/556778154461354/ ☞ Blocking of administrators will result in the removal of your posts and possibly you. ☞ No political or religion related posts....NO warnings will be given. This rule is non-negotiable (actually, NONE of them are negotiable) One or two word posts WILL be deleted, and the person posting will be muted (at least). Seriously, if you're unable to put together a full, coherent sentence, it's unlikely your "contribution" was worthy of being posted. NO comments such as "Who cares?" and the like. The goal here is to stimulate thoughtful and intelligent conversation. Attempts to stifle such conversation will not be looked upon kindly. If someone cared enough to post or comment, at least give them some small degree of consideration to what they're trying to communicate. Maybe YOU don't care, but there might be others out there that do. NO usage of the terms "Real fan", "True fan", or anything of the like. We ain't having a fuckin' competition in here to determine who the "greatest" fan is, folks. Yep, some of us are rabid fans, while others are more casual fans. ALL levels of Angels fans are to be respected at all times. Admins/mods reserve the right to impose additional rules/prohibitions in order to deal with problematic issues as they arise. For example, idiots commenting with "Can he pitch?" whenever a non-pitcher's name is mentioned, will earn a muting at the very least. USE YOUR COMMON SENSE in your posts and comments. Read your shit before you post it. If you think it might be offensive, stupid, or in violation of the above rules, you're probably right. In short, say most anything you want, but be prepared to back it up. Stupid fuckin' comments such as "He sucks" are pointless and idiotic. You wanna say someone sucks?....Then fine....But you better have something to back it up with besides venom. If you have ANY issue with a post please report it with a screenshot directly to the Admins listed below before using the FB option, failure to do this may result in your removal from the group. ADMINISTRATORS: JONATHAN ASHWORTH TONY PARADIS RALPH GIFFIN JOHN WOSCEK MODERATORS: ÅNGEL ZUBIÅ MATT ROGERS

                 Yoga for Mental Health w/ Ashley Turner
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WELCOME TO THE "Yoga for Mental Health by Ashley Turner" Private Group! The mission of this private group is to educate, empower + support yoga teaches, coaches, wellness/psychology professionals and students to improve mental health through an innovative fusion of yoga, science, psychology and spirituality. YOUR FIRST STEP: Visit the "Welcome New Members" UNIT and introduce yourself. Tell us who you are, where you're from, why you're here....ANNNDDD the #1 question you have (so I can address and answer them). I'M SO EXCITED TO HAVE YOU HERE! I'm devoted to helping yoga teachers, wellness leaders + soulful entrepreneurs THRIVE and build PROFITABLE businesses because you are doing some of the most important work on the planet! We need you building bigger businesses, making a bigger impact + unabashedly shining your LIGHT! –––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––––– Please read + follow these GROUND RULES: NO SELF PROMOTION This is a space of giving. Please DO NOT: • Sell products, services, courses, events, and programs • Promote a webinar, live broadcast, or event • Post affiliate links • Post your own content in the group and not in a specific (and relevant) thread • Post “free” offers of your own product or service • Once a week, we will create a "WEDNESDAY WIN" where you can share what you're up to + most proud of! BE KIND Please refrain from rants, criticisms and negativity. If you have a concern or complaint about one of Ashley's programs, please email info@AshleyTurner.org and we will handle it promptly. BE GENEROUS Provide genuine and helpful feedback, resources and suggestions to others. Be curious. Ask questions. Offer insight. Become the supportive, inspiring colleague you are seeking on your soulful business journey. STAY CONSISTENT Tune in every day to gain insight and knowledge. Dedicate a specific amount of time each day to your learning + growth! The seeds that grow are the seeds you water. SCHEDULE IT (one of THE biggest tips for entrepreneurs!) Ashley will be live on video inside this group most Fridays. These live sessions will be recorded and accessible later in the FB LIVE UNIT, but, we highly recommend you show up LIVE to share in and contribute to the magic (and even get a chance to spontaneously jump on LIVE for some LASER COACHING with Ashley). Mark your calendar and make it a habit to join us live, if possible! We are all on this journey + here to uplevel together! Sending massive love + so happy to have you here, Ashley

                 This group is designed to help you sell your high quality cycling gear and help with any bicycle related questions members have. Feel free to join and post on N+1 Bicycles buy/sell/trade https://www.facebook.com/groups/NPLUS1Bicycles/ -Please be respectful at all times. Please be respectful at all times. Please be respectful at all times. -No stock photos of items you’re selling. Actual photos of the item required. -No big-box-store bike brands! -Do not post any spam here. -Do not promote your business here. -Do not share listings/posts from other groups/pages. *sharing eBay listings is ok IF it’s a $1 starting price no reserve auction. -We do allow sponsored posts. Are you planning on promoting a business or selling inventory of a business? Contact admin (Stephen W) for details. -Any person selling stolen or counterfeit items will be reported and blocked -Be kind and courteous when interacting with fellow cyclists, if you have a post you would like to report please do so, and I will review it. Do not publicly bash other members. -This group has grown from a small local group in California to a group with many members across the country so remember, all the information you can post about your item and where its located is helpful. Thanks for posting! -All members can post in this group. Bicyclevalues.com, admins, and moderators are not responsible or guarantee the content of members posts. -This is a free market group. All transactions are between individual seller and buyer. We will not be involved in any transactions. It’s your responsibility you protect yourself. What is Bicyclevalues.com? (1) It’s a Math formula that I’ve used for years to help calculate what a used bike is worth. (2) We work with Bicycle shops, Manufactures, Race teams.... when they have inventory that they would like to liquidate. It could be 10 bikes or 500+. (3) We buy used bicycles as well. Feel free to fill out the trade-in form on our website to receive a cash offer for your used bike. The trade-in price is typically 35% less than the market value for your used bike.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Boxing: The Sweet Science
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING** This is a group for Boxing fans. We discuss Boxing. Not MMA, not politics, not football....BOXING. There are a few rules in this group which we take very seriously. Breaking any of these will get you booted: - NO SPAM. Not for your group. Not for your blog. Not for your podcast. We are not a farm for your clicks. It kills banter and we won't tolerate it. If there is a charitable cause or a book or something you'd really like to share, send me a link and we will consider it. - NO TROLLS. If you make negative comments based on someones religion, race, gender or sexual orientation, EFF OFF. (We also don't like the "R" word. I can't even bring myself to type it - neither should you.) - Threats of violence are unacceptable, and will result in an immediate nuking. Challenging people to fight because you disagree with their opinion is included in this. - WE ARE NOT WORLDSTARR. Do not post street fight videos here. They will be deleted, as will you. Repeated posts about the same topic is discouraged. Please check to see if someone has already posted something and then JOIN THE CONVERSATION. Please chill on the fantasy match-ups, personal p4p lists and personal workout videos - we've kind of run the gamut on those already. Fantastic group etiquette includes: - Treating people with dignity and respect - even if you disagree with them - If you are unable to do so at first, come back and apologize / make peace. This goes a long way. - Join conversations and get to know other group members. That's why we are here!! - Bring your best. Analysis, scorecard, boxing news, boxing memes - BRING IT. I started this group with a handful of people and we have opened the group to find more awesome people to talk boxing with, but if we don't get along with you, your time here will be short. This is NOT A DEMOCRACY - it is a boxing group run by a handful of people and it does matter if we like you. SorryNotSorry. Let's keep it about boxing and enjoy the banter, people!! WARNING: Casual fans may be ripped a new anus, but will eventually be embraced into the fold. (That doesn't sound as awesome as it actually is.)
                </div>

This is not a place for religion, politics or other personal beliefs unrelated to yoga. If you would't talk about it at your yoga studio, it's not appropriate here either. This also goes for the way in which you speak with and speak to other members. If your post or comment has been deleted it is not personal. It just means that it is not the type of subject matter that is welcome in this safe, respectful, and positive group. Thank you so much for your understanding. This group is brought to you by YogiApproved.com and I LOVE YOGA Please keep it to positive vibes only. Namaste.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 49ER EMPIRE
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The 49er Empire, also referred to as The Niner Empire, was founded in the mid-1990s after NFL Hall of Fame coach John Madden quoted the San Francisco 49ers as being, "The Roman Empire of the NFL". The 49er Empire has an established reputation as the extreme and hostile faction of the original 49er fan base, the 49er Faithful. With their adrenalin-rushed intensity, the 49er Empire counters the old stereotype of the 49er "wine-and-cheese" fans. They encourage all 49er fans to show their intense loyalty and are often recognized as the more vocal members in and around the stadium, often breaking into enthusiastically-driven, loud outbursts in unison and party-animal-style tailgates. Since their inception, a new generation of 49er fans have adapted to the 49er Empire movement as chapters and booster groups align allegiance across the globe. Today, regardless of the San Francisco 49ers' decline from glory, the San Francisco 49er fans that comprise the 49er Empire continue to multiply and are always found at Levi Stadium demonstrating their extreme loyalty to their team. Founder: Jay Esperanza (AJ CERTIFIED) Group Moderators: Mario Zazueta &amp; Tay Porter

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A place to Buy , Sell, or Trade or just share information about ALPINE SNOWBOARD EQUIPMENT! FYI, Have you been turned away? DID YOU ANSWER THE QUESTIONS? Do you have anything in your profile indicating you are interested in Alpine Snowboarding? In an effort to keep the group focus we are careful to keep out those not about Alpine Snowboarding OK? You are welcome to post info about alpine events, tips and tricks info or help questions. Rules You must be a member of AST to buy, sell or trade. COMMUNICATE!!! politely please, include the who, what, where, why etc in your original post. Please use an honest 10 scale and describe any damages. This is a family page, however by FB rules you must be 18 yrs.old to join. Do not use foul language! Your post Will be deleted!!! First words in your post should always be capitalized and include: BUY , SELL, TRADE, ESTIMATE, AUCTION , IF the snowboard equipment is more than approx. 10 years old please add the word "VINTAGE" to make clear it is directed to the collectors. Second sentence should include what it is you are selling, boards, bindings, boots etc. PLEASE avoid third party links (eBay) unless it's a screaming local Craigslist deal and you're willing to pick &amp; ship. Also- Alpine and BX boards only please - we will tolerate limited amounts of freestyle gear, but there are plenty of other groups for that, and we would like to focus on Alpine and BX. Be a good member, help this promote the sport, promote kindness. Then go out and RIP a Fine Line!!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Mental Training Tips for Swimmers and Swim Coaches
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 🏊 🏊 🏊 Welcome to this private group for competitive swimmers and swim coaches! This is your home for proven and time-tested strategies that you can use to maximize your mindset in the water. The group is managed by Olivier Poirier-Leroy, former national level swimmer, Olympic Trials qualifier, and author of “Conquer the Pool: The Swimmer’s Ultimate Guide for a High-Performance Mindset.” The book is used by some of the top teams and swimmers on the planet, including Olympic gold medalists and NCAA champions. Over the years he has helped thousands of swimmers clear the mental clutter so that they can perform their best. This group is all about helping you improve your mindset. Whether it’s getting mentally tough, improving your self-talk, learning how to stay focused on the process, or using visualization to nail your race-day preparation, we got you covered. Some basic ground rules: 🚫 Self-promotion is not permitted in the group. Please stay on topic. If you want help with your stroke or to find a cool new pair of goggles, there are other resources on FB (and Google). Off-topic posts will be deleted, and repeat offenders will be removed from the group. Got a question? Don’t be shy--ask! This group is for discussion and sharing tips. If there is something you want help with, want feedback on, or you have a killer tip for your fellow swimmers and swim coaches, by all means share. CONNECT: Olivier writes a weekly newsletter for competitive swimmers that goes into deeper detail about some of the mental strategies discussed here. ➡️ You can subscribe for free here: https://www.yourswimlog.com/newsletter/ ➡️ For more information on Conquer the Pool: The Swimmer’s Ultimate Guide for a High-Performance Mindset: https://www.yourswimlog.com/conquer-the-pool/ Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/yourswimbook Twitter: https://www.twitter.com/yourswimbook 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Promoting a greater awareness of Joseph Pilates’ time interned on the Isle of Man, 100+ years after he was interned at Knockaloe Internment Camp. Rules for this Group 1: There will be no cursing in this group – ever. That also includes any statement that the administrator deems inappropriate in nature. 2: Do not advertise items for sale on this group. If you wish to advertise your services or an event please ask the administrator first. 3: All opinions will be treated with mutual respect, unless they violate the group rules. Treat your fellow Facebook group members with that same respect. 4: If a single individual starts a discussion that all other members disagree with, it may, at the discretion of the administrator, be removed. 5: If a member personally attacks another member with words that are harmful, threatening or not in-line with our mutual respect policy, that member will be removed from the group. 6: Please stick to the mission statement of this Facebook group. Irrelevant content does not belong here it belongs on other pages. 7: Do not post inappropriate photos, videos and other media in this group. If you are not sure about the content that you want to post, email the administrator. 8: If someone posts a comment that is inflammatory please report it to the administrator. 9: Think before you post! This is Facebook, one of the biggest sites on the internet – what goes up can never really come down. Respect the privacy of others! 10: It is considered impolite to re-post or draw attention to the fact that a group admin or another member has deleted your comment. 11: If you are going to comment, be friendly, fair, honest and make sure your comments are justified. 12: The Administrator is entitled to deny entry to any member they choose. They are also allowed to remove members that don’t comply with the aforementioned rules. 13: The administrator’s decision is final. Group administrator J Grubb.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Greater Los Angeles Cycling Buy &amp; Sell FB Page
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello All, this is an open group for those of you who are looking for a platform to trade, buy, or sell your cycling related items. Please keep in mind that this page merely serves as a "marketplace", each individual is responsible for themselves when conducting any transaction. No one is responsible for you. If you're left unhappy with your transaction, you're responsible for it. Here are some basic rules, please follow them accordingly: 1) Please buy, sell, or trade on cycling related items only. 2) Please list your price, this applies to all posts; posting a photo with only the word "offer" is just simply lazy. All posts seeking offers will be removed. 3) Please have photos with your post. 4) Please wait a minimum of 3 days before you "bump" your post to the top of the page. There are reasons behind unsold items; no need to force others to look at your post over and over. 5) Keep all communication between buyer and seller to private messaging. 6) Be clear and concise to what you're selling. i.e size, specs, condition, known &amp; suspected issues, make &amp; model, or any additional information that pertains to your item. 7) If you are looking to trade your items with something else, please describe what you would like to trade and what you're offering for trade. This page will not tolerate any post with poor information. 8) Once your items are sold, please comment the item as sold. 9) Be respectful to the rules of this page. 10) Be respectful towards others. New for 2017: A) Helmets, must have a picture of the manufacturing dates accompanying the post. Considering typical helmets have lifespan of 3-year. This is an important safety concern. and last but not least, this is for all of you who are selling on this page, if you do not respond to potential buyers' inquiries within 48 hours the moderators will consider your item as sold, and will remove the post from the page. best of luck, Below is a link from Pinkbike.com which contains plenty of useful tips for buying and selling online. please read through it carefully as it will help you, and should protect you from potentially trouble transactions. http://www.pinkbike.com/forum/listcomments/?threadid=113294 Useful Links: Bike Theft Database https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSdJjO-4oFgxd4Ltyjo8cwZAH2HHi8E4a6QwM1MXqozHZ4U1aQ/viewform
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Emerging Cricket Forum - Fans for an Expanded World Cup
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group dedicated to sharing and discussing news and views of the emerging cricket world - and advocating for further development of the game beyond the Full Members of the ICC. The fundamental element that originally brought the group together was the ICC’s decision to reduce the Cricket World Cup to 10 teams despite the great success of the 14 team 2015 event. With the addition of Afghanistan and Ireland as Full Members there’s an even slimmer chance of Associate nations qualifying for the sport’s pinnacle event and the common thread that unites this group’s members is the firm belief this decision should be reversed and that the ICC should be looking at increasing the numbers from 14 not reducing them. Please keep all discussion respectful and reasoned. Any spam / abuse or any vilification will result in posts deleted and users blocked from the group.

                 LEXI'S LOYAL LEGIONS- Fans of LPGA Golfer Lexi Thompson
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This page is for FANS of LPGA golfer Lexi Thompson. All who share admiration for this wonderfully talented young lady are welcome to join and share their thoughts, comments, and pictures. We especially welcome comments from any of you who are fortunate enough to have actually met Lexi. This is NOT a site for advertisements or solicitations of ANY kind. I am a free market capitalist and I welcome and celebrate anyone’s entrepreneurial spirit, but create your own page. I will delete any advertisements as soon as they are reported to me. This is NOT a site for criticism of Lexi, any other golfers, or the LPGA. If you have some specific, CONSTRUCTIVE criticism of her performance on the course, and if you are capable of expressing those comments in a respectful manner, then you may do so. As administrator, I reserve the right to delete any comments or criticisms I deem to be offensive, or too personal. NO COMMENTS OF AN EXPLICIT OR SEXUAL NATURE WILL BE PERMITTED, AND ANY VIOLATION OF THIS POLICY WILL RESULT IN IMMEDIATE EXPULSION AND BLOCKING FROM THIS SITE!!!!! I have no reason to believe that Lexi has ever seen or will ever see this site. However, on the off chance the she might, at some point, have this site brought to her attention, I want her to know that this is a page she can come to where she can hear from and possibly (if she chooses) interact with her fans. I reiterate, this is a site for FANS of Lexi. If you don’t like her, for whatever reasons, that is your right. You are free to create your very own “I Hate Lexi” page and recruit all the like-minded people you wish. However, derogatory comments ARE NOT WELCOME HERE!!! Let’s have fun with our common admiration for Lexi Thompson. WELCOME ABOARD, LEXI’S LOYAL LEGIONS!!! Michael Rochen, Administrator

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Where have all the bowling alleys gone?
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Sometime in the mid 70's I was introduced to my first bowling alley. Most likely it was Maple Lanes in Brooklyn, NY. My earliest memories are of being in the day care area downstairs from the lanes while my mom bowled in her afternoon league. Bowling has become a life long obsession. In 2013 Maple Lanes will close it's doors forever, a Brooklyn bowling institution which touched the lives of thousands of people over the last 50 years. This story has been repeated hundreds if not thousands of times over the last two decades throughout the United States. Hundreds of bowling alleys have succumbed to the realities of urban redevelopment, real estate boom, small business erosion, government bureaucracy and the technological revolution which has consumed millions of hours of our time, mostly in the convenience of our home. Bowling thrived in the urban blue collar communities of the 40's, 50's and 60's. During that time hundreds of bowling alleys and thousands of lanes cropped up all over America. This group is dedicated to memory of these great establishments which gave so many of us entertainment and life long friendships throughout the twentieth century
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">7,108 位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">0 篇新帖</span></span>
                </div>

                 SportsTalk365
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for fans of ALL sports! This is predominantly a debate group. So, please try to keep the trash talk to a minimum bc we want as much *real talk* as possible! Whenever you think someone is full of bs, just say *real talk* and all should be rational! Let's be fans to talk all of sports first before homering!. You must be 18+ to be in here. This is an adult group! New members, please post upon entry &amp; state your teams! Our motto is, "Quality over Quantity." ⭐⭐Rules⭐⭐ 1) NO TROLLING on main topic threads or game threads! Keep the trolling for the obvious troll threads! 2) Sports related topics only (NSR only after major seasons are over)! 3) No profile Digging (Using others pics for memes, etc)! 4) No racist talk, No Religion, &amp; No Politics! 5) If someone bothers you, grow thick skin, or BLOCK them! 6) No advertising of any sort! (Promoting other groups, websites, etc) If you want to advertise a group or page, pm admin first to make sure it's approved of! 7) No personal attacks or attacking family or loved ones of other members! 8) No reporting! If caught, you will be banned! Tag or take it up with admin! 9) No calling out ppl on the main board for whatever reason(s). This is NOT a SMACK group! If you feel the need, keep it in the thread &amp; not for ALL to see! Think before you act! 10) No Blocking Admin! We can still see what you're saying &amp; doing! Other than that, this is group designed for fans who can do *real talk* instead of always insulting, bashing, talking smack, or constantly trash talking. MOST of us are here bc we're TIRED of ALL SMACK groups! Trash talking &amp; SMACK are two totally different things! Yea, trash talk is inevitable. Rules don't have to be broken to be booted. As long as you're a productive member in a positive manner, there's no need to worry. Admin do not boot just bc they disagree with you. In other words, we tend to our garden (the group) to deweed the bad from the good to maintain quality! Please try to keep the memes in threads away until the end or until the thread is dying. If you encounter rules being broken (over the top), please tag admin &amp; lookout for the best interest of the group. We're not able to catch everything &amp; we don't want to lose any good members bc they couldn't tag or pm administration. Trolling is ok as long as you don't only come in here to troll every single time &amp; only if you keep it in obvious troll threads. If you can't bring any merit or knowledge to this group (other than trolling), you will be shown the exit! Please RESPECT others at the end of the day. Agree to disagree! This is a CLOSED group! So, whatever you say will not show up anywhere else or on anybody else's news feed. Please feel free to post whatever sports related. Invite your friends as well &amp; Enjoy the best sports group on Facebook!! Thanks to all bc you guys &amp; gals are the reason why this is such a great group!!

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 READ RULES BELOW... A place to share skills, drills, and any ideas for helping our athletes improve. Let's see that new drill, or the new skills your athletes are working that none of your other friends understand! Group Rules: 1. Use the correct post type. Nearly 100% of all post are 'regular discussion type posts. Do not use 'Looking for Recommendations ' post type, as it makes commenting cumbersome and difficult. 2. Keep the forum clutter-free. Do not use fancy backgrounds on your posts. Plain old boring text ONLY. 3. Be BOLD. This group should have a bit of the wild-wild-west. If you have an opinion, state it. At the same time, if you have an opinion, expect that someone may challenge it. However, civil discourse is required. See lengthy debate notes below (coming soon... too long for the top of these rules). 4. Keep discussions IN THIS GROUP. Do NOT solicit people to send you private messages, or to post their email address. This group discussion benefits more than just the people posting and commenting. There are thousands of people who actually read the dialog, and learn from it. Keep discussions in this group. 5. NO BLOCKING ADMINS. This will result in an instant BAN from this group. 6. Please keep the document sharing IN THIS GROUP, and not via email. To share a document, simply make a new post, and choose the file tab / option. Describe your file in the post text, and you will be prompted to choose the file from your local computer, and it will be uploaded to that post. At that point, it will appear in this group as a new post, with a file attachment, for all here to benefit. 7. Do NOT use animated GIFs in comments. And, the rules keep getting longer and longer... for those that don't get it... Clarification of Rules There are NO restrictions on commenting on posts. If you're an ass, and you comment like an ass, everybody will know something about you... your an ass. Telling people that they are only allowed to comment on your post, if they support your idea, coaching philosophy, method of coaching, etc, is NOT acceptable. You are allowed to call out the post and comments, with critical comments and rebuttals. This group is NOT about: Adult Sexual Activity Sexual Orientation Politics This group IS about: Gymnastics Coaching Gymnastics Skills Gymnastics Drills

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Storm/Roto Grip Bowling Balls For Sale Aka SRGBBFS. This is where people buy, trade and sell Storm/Roto grip bowling balls, shoes, apparel, bags etc. If you would like to show off your Storm/Roto Grip collection. Show off your recently purchased Storm/Roto Grip bowling balls. Brag about your games with Storm/Roto Grip bowling balls. Post your honor scores with Storm/Roto Grip bowling balls. You might even find a discontinued ball that you have been looking for a while! We also do plenty of giveaways! GROUP RULES: 1. No price police, if you don't like the price please move along. 2. Do not post other companies products for sale. Your post will be deleted. 3. Please be respectful to your fellow group members. 4. Please include a clear picture and price, for any and all sales. 5. Post if your bowling ball is new in box, 1st drill, 2nd drill etc. 6. Please post if your product has sold so people are aware it’s no longer available. 7. Do not post about a trade for any other company besides Storm/Roto Grip or your post will be deleted.. however you may pm each other about trades if it's not storm/Roto Grip. 8. Foul language is not allowed in posts. 9. Once you have been notified about your post. You will have 1 hour to fix the issue or it will be removed. 10. No hijacking posts. 11. Please post a picture of every item that is being sold. 12. Multiple posts about other brand balls for sale or trade you will be removed from the group. 13. Post a actual picture of the product being sold. (Not one from the internet) 14. Drawings can only be ran by a admin. 15. there will be no promoting other brands in this group. 16. Any leaked information will be removed. 17. No bashing each other. We are all here to have fun!! *If you would like to host a giveaway. Please consult with Nick Brown before posting. Any and all giveaways posted before contacting us will be removed.* (This includes ball giveaways, apparel giveaways, and YouTube giveaways.) SRGBBFS Merchandise: www.LogoInfusion.com/SRGBBFS Code: SRGBBFS for 25% off! CONTACT INFORMATION: If you have any questions about the group or members in the group please feel free to contact one of our team members. Email: srgbbfs@yahoo.com Our Facebook page: https://m.facebook.com/srgbbfs/ Visit our facebook page. Our facebook page is for updates on new products featuring the Storm/Roto Grip/Master brands! Sponsors: Logo Infusion Inc. Website (www.LogoInfusion.com) Coupon code: SRGBBFS for 25% OFF any order!
